class="or os gu bf ot ou ov ow ox oy oz pa pb pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj pk pl pm pn po bk">Executive Summary</h1><ul class=""><li id="8481" class="mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt pu pv pw bk">BlackGuard Stealer, which collects and exfiltrates credentials and device information from infected PC, first appeared when the official seller posted a promotion article on the dark web forum in January 2022</li><li id="9d3a" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt pu pv pw bk">BlackGuard Stealer collects and exfiltrates not only credentials such as Browser user data, Local files, Crypto wallets, VPN accounts, Steam accounts, Discord tokens, FileZilla data, and Telegram session data, but also device information such as OS version, System information, IPv4, country, and screenshot from infected PC</li><li id="2ce3" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt pu pv pw bk">The collected information is stored in a temporarily created folder. After collecting information, the folder is compressed to a *.zip file and exfiltrated through Telegram API.</li></ul><h1 id="c718" class="or os gu bf ot ou ov ow ox oy oz pa pb pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj pk pl pm pn po bk">Introduction of BlackGuard Stealer</h1><p id="9a75" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">BlackGuard is one of the info stealers written in C#. It is mostly distributed through malicious software disguised as Windows Update file, Fake MS Office Installer, Computer cleaner software, etc.</p><p id="6ad2" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk">Recently, the info stealer abused the description of a YouTube video by attaching the download link that contains the info stealer. In March 2022, a link to download a game hack program was posted in the YouTube video description, but when users downloaded and ran the software, 44Caliber Stealer was executed on the users’ PC.</p><figure class="ob oc od oe of og ny nz paragraph-image"><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="oh oi fj oj bh ok"><div class="ny nz qc"><picture><source my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt pu pv pw bk">Reference: <a class="af oq" href="https://asec.ahnlab.com/en/32499/" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" https[:]//anonfiles[.]com/J0b03cKexf</li></ul><p id="dcde" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk">BlackGuard Stealer, which is currently being distributed, is forked from 44Caliber Stealer. Both BlackGuard and 44Caliber use the same method to collect credentials and device information. In addition, they store them in a temporarily created folder and compress them to the *.zip file. But while BlackGuard uses Telegram’s <strong class="my gv">sendDocument</strong> API, 44Caliber uses Discord Webhook API to exfiltrate.</p><h1 id="f5a1" class="or os gu bf ot ou ov ow ox oy oz pa pb pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj pk pl pm pn po bk">Timeline of BlackGuard Stealer</h1><p id="8c9d" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">Since it first appeared on the dark web forum in January 2022, BlackGuard Stealer has been updated its builder and web panel. In particular, considering that the proportion of samples discovered from March 2022 is increasing, it can be seen that BlackGuard Stealer is currently active.</p><figure class="ob oc od oe of og ny update was on February 9, 2022. At that time, Wallet extensions of Chrome and Edge, Edge Beta were added, and the types of collected information became more diverse.</p><h1 id="bbc1" class="or os gu bf ot ou ov ow ox oy oz pa pb pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj pk pl pm pn po bk">BlackGuard Stealer on DDW</h1><p id="6972" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">The user with the nicknames “BlackGUARD07” and “blackteam007” posted a Stealer promotion article in Russian-based forums, XSS and BHF, in January 2022. BlackGuard Stealer Execution Flow</h2><ol class=""><li id="0eb1" class="mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt qv pv pw bk">When the loader is executed, BlackGuard Stealer is dropped and executed.</li><li id="0ea6" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt qv pv pw bk"><strong class="my gv">Help &amp; Config Data</strong> are decoded and then used for collecting and exfiltrating credentials and device information.</li><li id="0640" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt qv pv pw bk">Anti Debugging: Checks the existence of DnSpy, a tool used for decompiling .NET assembly, and whether it is currently being debugged.</li><li id="61e3" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt qv pv pw bk">Collects credentials and device information from infected PC and stores them in the <strong class="my gv">ChikenDir</strong> folder specified in <strong class="my gv">Help Data.</strong></li><li id="b296" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt qv pv pw bk">Compresses <strong class="my gv">ChikenDir</strong> to the zip file.</li><li id="1c78" class="mw mx gu my b mz px nb nc nd py nf ng nh pz nj nk nl qa nn no np qb nr ns nt qv pv pw bk">Exfiltrates the zip file through dy ox qj qk ea pb nh ql qm qn nl qo qp qq np qr qs qt qu bk">3. Decode Help &amp; Config Data</h2><p id="8459" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">In the BlackGuard Stealer, the data used for collecting and exfiltrating credentials and device information are hard-coded. <strong class="my gv">Help Data</strong> is used to collect and includes system directory paths, the <strong class="my gv">ChikenDir</strong> folder path, and device information. Config data is mainly used to exfiltrate collected information through Telegram API and includes Telegram Bot Token, Chat ID, and keywords for collecting files. Most of the data inside these classes are base64-encoded and gzip-compressed.</p><p id="cb72" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt Anti Debugging</h2><p id="cffb" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">Before BlackGuard collects credentials and device information, it uses Anti Debugging methods. It detects the decompiler by checking if the “dnSpy.xml” file exists, and uses “Sleep()” and “DateTime.Now.Ticks” to determine whether it is being debugged.</p><h2 id="baf3" class="qg os gu bf ot qh qi dy ox qj qk ea pb nh ql qm qn nl qo qp qq np qr qs qt qu bk">5. Collect Credentials and Device Information</h2><p id="64e4" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk">BlackGuard Stealer collects Browser user data, Local files, Crypto wallets, VPN, Steam, Discord, FileZilla, Telegram, system information, and screenshot. Every time each piece of information is collected, the number of information is counted and stored separately. The collected data stored in the <strong class="my gv">ChikenDir</strong> folder is shown in the figure below.</p><figure class="ob oc od oe of og ny nz paragraph-image"><div role="button" gv">Browsers Folder</strong></p><p id="06d8" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk">In the <em class="nx">Browsers</em> folder, each browsers’ user data is stored. A subfolder is created for each type of browser, and the collected user data is saved as *.txt files in each folder. While Chrome and Edge browsers’ user data includes CC, Password, Cookie, History, Downloads, and AutoFill, and Gecko-based browsers additionally collect logins.json, which contains login information, qq np qr qs qt qu bk">6. Exfiltrate Information</h2><p id="d563" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz pp nb nc nd pq nf ng nh pr nj nk nl ps nn no np pt nr ns nt gn bk"><strong class="my gv">Compress the folder to the *.zip file</strong></p><p id="8640" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk">BlackGuard compresses the ChikenDir folder that contains collected information to the zip file and exfiltrates it to the Telegram C2 Server. The name format of zip file is <strong class="my gv">[HWID]([Current Date]).zip</strong></p><p id="a581" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk"><strong class="my gv">Telegram Bot API</strong></p><p id="0479" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mw mx gu my b mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn no np nq nr ns nt gn bk">BlackGuard sets up Telegram Bot URL to exfiltrate the zip file and send it using <strong class="my gv">sendDocument</strong> API with POST method. The data sent together includes the number of collected information for each type, the collected target software list, and the list of detected target domains. The message body sent to the Telegram Bot is as shown below.</p><figure class="ob oc od oe of og ny nz paragraph-image"><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="oh oi fj oj bh ok"><div class="ny nz
